&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">三、本期获悉狱中<span lang="EN-US">20</span>人的动态信息（附简历）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、徐光、陈剑雄、何宗旺<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被判刑：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">七、</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本期中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">1727</span>名在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引</span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日共收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3289</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">8</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">八年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">八年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网邮箱：</span></b></span><a href="mailto:wqw2011@gmail.com"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">wqw2011@gmail.com</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">103</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整八年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">5</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">9</span>千字</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">38</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">46</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">49</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1727</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk159649535"></a><a name="_Hlk507373498"></a><a class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨任涛、于桂兰、曾跃玲、张勤、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>张伟、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵作媛、钟义芳、陈煜、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"></span><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk165076209">别克什·马铁甫汗</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">哈萨克族，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，新疆阿尔泰市人，阿尔泰市布尔津县奥伊玛克乡卡台村公民，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">BikeshManapqan</span>，哈萨克族企业家，中国在押维权人士。自中共政府对新疆维吾尔自治区各少数族裔采取愈加严苛的管理以来，其所在阿尔泰市布尔津县成为新疆当局“扫黑除恶专项行动”的重灾区（之一），期间，其全家（含其父亲和两个兄长等）因在布尔津县喀纳斯湖风景区经办了一家知名的旅游公司，不仅为其家族赚得了较多收入，也为当地旅游业的发展提供了不小的便利，随被地方当局看重和欲加掠夺；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，阿尔泰地区布尔津县当局曾多次派人与其父等人谈判，试图以贿赂的方式让其放弃对喀纳斯湖风景区旅游公司的全部经营权，后被其拒绝，随遭记恨与迫害；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其被布尔津县奥伊玛克乡警方突然带走，直接送到当地一家“再教育营”关押，自此失联；后因其不愿接受“再教育营”对其的洗脑式培训，同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，遂与其父亲及两个哥哥被阿尔泰市布尔津县警方借“扫黑除恶”之名，以涉嫌“非法经营罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”等转为刑拘；后又被布尔津县检察院以涉嫌以同罪名正式批捕，指控其等数人因参与“暴力行为、敲诈勒索和霸凌行为、强征管理费、大肆打架、寻衅滋事、妨碍公务程序、参与喀纳斯旅游景区违法经营”等行为，触犯了国家的相关法律和规定，遂应予以逮捕、判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其一行多人“涉黑恶势力”案在阿尔泰市布尔津县法院统一开庭受审，其中，其被以“非法经营罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月；据悉，其家人之前一直无其更多讯息，直到<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其妻子在一篇《扫黑除恶：布尔钦县首例公开汇编涉嫌“黑势力”案件》的官方文章中，才发现了其被判刑的具体信息。目前疑似在新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰市福海监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/7.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">佳木斯法轮功学员。佳木斯市东风区建国乡群力村村民。一九九七年幸开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始对法轮功的残酷迫害后，程玉兰多次遭受迫害，曾经一度被迫流离失所、有家难回。程玉兰于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被佳木斯前进公安分局国保大队入室抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被佳木斯向阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，罚金一万，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/14/458788.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、冯颖军：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底，被海淀区清河派出所警察抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/26/446805.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">4</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: 0pt;">、高婵玲：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西省忻州市代县法轮功女学员，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生。在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点许，遭受到代县公安局<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名警察抄家、抓捕；家中的电脑、打印机、大法书籍、及私人存折都被洗劫。当天，至少有<span lang="EN-US">11</span>名法轮功学员被抓捕、抄家抢劫，被强迫录像、拍照、采血、签字、写保证。高婵玲先被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，随后就被转入代县洗脑班进行迫害，高压逼迫她签写“四书”，高婵玲坚决抵制，后又被抓捕到忻州市看守所关押构陷迫害，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并且罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445961.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk165076392">郝虎成</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生，河北省邯郸市武安市活水乡马店头村人，法轮功学员。在北京市以修理空调电器为生。郝虎城曾于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年在浙江宁波打工期间向世人讲述法轮功真相时被抓捕，被浙江省宁波法院判刑两年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年期间，郝虎城通过微信向（大纪元）记者发送了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>段拜年视频。正月初<span lang="EN-US">6</span>，北京市国保警察通过微信软件及收寄快递地址定位后电话联系了郝虎城，由于正月期间郝虎城回原籍老家过年，北京市国保责令武安市活水乡派出所对郝虎城实施管控。活水乡派出所遂签发了对郝虎城拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天的拘留证，因郝虎城提出要请北京律师复议，派出所未执行拘留。农历<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初，郝虎城再次去北京打工。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，郝虎城在北京市城区开汽车途中，遭警察手机定位拦截、搜查，警察从郝虎城的车里发现了<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>张<span lang="EN-US">5</span>元面值的真相币，然后闯到郝虎城的租住屋中将郝虎城的手机、存折等私人物品抄走。当晚，郝虎城被抓捕至北京市昌平区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，北京市昌平区法院判决郝虎城<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/28/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E6%AD%A6%E5%AE%89%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%83%9D%E8%99%8E%E5%9F%8E%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441846.html"><span _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk165076516">贾乃芝</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁抚顺市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生。贾乃芝一九九七年十一月开始修炼法轮功。自一九九九年七月二十日中共江泽民集团开始疯狂迫害法轮功，二十多年来，贾乃芝遭受的残酷迫害数不胜数，多次被抓捕，被羁押在拘留所、自强学校、教养院、看守所、监狱，长时间过着暗无天日的生活，多种酷刑迫害，身心受到严酷的摧残，累计冤狱十多年，自由被剥夺，财产被抢去，受邪恶政策株连，善良的丈夫承受不住压力被迫离婚，年迈的母亲长期思念女儿不得见，含泪而死，孩子得不到妈妈的照顾，遭遇二十多年的迫害，使贾乃芝夫离子散，家破人亡。贾乃芝<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日再次被抓捕，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被关押到辽宁女子监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月期间检查出肝病大三阳（传染期）。贾乃芝的家属给辽宁女子监狱狱警打了电话，了解一下贾乃芝的身体情况，监狱并没有给贾乃芝医治，家属要求保外就医，监狱狱警说，办不了。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US">22</span>年中，累计被监禁<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">59</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，李银欢被广州市公安局、长兴派出所警察从家中抓捕，被关押在天河区看守所。李银欢被关押和构陷一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，被海珠区法院开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，李银欢被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚金六千元。从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月开始，广州社保停发了她的养老金。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/29/462468.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/29/462468.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">11</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、林乐宏：女，</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1976</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，大学本科毕业，家住深圳市南山区。林乐宏和马彦平都暂在深圳龙岗区布吉镇大芬油画村租住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上，林乐宏、马彦平在大芬油画村租住房内，被龙岗区公安分局国保及布吉派出所警察抓捕，并被抄家，两人被关押到龙岗区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，警察再次对<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人的租住房进行了查抄，将法轮功书籍、资料、电脑、打印机、塑封机、切边机、硬盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等个人物品全部劫走。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，林乐宏、马彦平被龙岗区检察院批捕。被关押后，林乐宏多次绝食反迫害，遭看守所强制灌食，健康受到严重伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，林乐宏被强制灌食后，被送医院所谓“抢救”。从此，林乐宏吃什么吐什么，回到看守所后，身体<span lang="EN-US">1</span>直不好。血压高至<span lang="EN-US">160/180mmHg</span>（低血压高）。她每周需要吸氧<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次，只能吃流食，出现心口痛，左手麻木。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，林乐宏、马彦平被盐田区法院庭审。有律师出庭做无罪辩护。为了抵制持续的迫害，从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日始，林乐宏又开始绝食，被连续强制灌食<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多天。体重只剩<span lang="EN-US">46</span>公斤，舌根发硬，吞咽困难，胸口时常发闷，血糖极低（不到<span lang="EN-US">3mmol/L</span>），手脚冰凉，特别怕冷，<span lang="EN-US">26</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">︒</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">C</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">的气温下还要穿大棉袄。在林乐宏身体健康严重受损的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，盐田区法院宣判，林乐宏被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；马彦平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk165076836">刘朋</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北石家庄市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁，石家庄市长安区人。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日与女儿王炳程被居住地派出所和长安公安分局抓捕，母女后被转入石家庄市第二看守所关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，桥西区法院对其母女二人均判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk165076875">马纳普汗（哈萨克）</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆阿尔泰地区哈萨克族居民，哈萨克族良心犯、人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，因其获得一本从哈萨克斯坦国带回的《古兰经》，所以被当地公安局将其一家三口悉数抓走，并被指控“持有非法宗教出版物”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其“持古兰经案”被当地法院开庭审理，一家三口分别被以“持有非法宗教出版物罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。开庭前，其要求聘请律师遭拒。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk165076913">马秀云</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京市朝阳区法轮功学员。唐平顺，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年六十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因发大法真相资料被关押三十天，后又被劫持到洗脑班迫害。妻子马秀云，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年六十多岁，多次被关押、劳教。唐平顺、马秀云夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日再次被警察抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夫妻二人均被朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金四千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/1/461495.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/1/461495.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">17</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、孟凯：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1970</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年代出生，湖北省人，长沙市某公司法务工作者，自由信仰追求者，法轮功修炼者，中国在押良心犯。早期曾就读于武汉华中农业大学法律系，毕业后成为一名执业律师，并曾参加研究生考试；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年起，中共开始迫害法轮功，因其信仰和练习法轮功，并曾将<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>张法轮功宣传数据从湖南长沙带到岳阳进行宣传，随被“<span lang="EN-US">601</span>”发监管办公室监控人员举报、刑拘，后被湖南省岳阳市法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；获释后，因其全家搬到长沙市，其随家人一同亦迁至长沙市居住；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其开始在一家公司做法务工作，并因平日工作敬业，积极为公司解决了许多搁置已久、悬而未决的事项，从而获得公司法务部总管及同事们的普遍赞扬；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其在前往外地帮公司打官司的途中，突遭湖南省浏阳市警方抓捕，后得知亦有另<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余名法轮功信仰者（含多名博士生、高干、律师等各类人士）同期均被湖南省长沙市当局以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘；次日，其旋即又被以同罪名转正式逮捕，且被关押在长沙市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其家属及代理律师知其已被秘密判刑，刑期不清；据悉，因其拒绝认罪，负责其案的警方曾称，“这个态度要判他<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年”；其代理律师请求与其会见，遭拒，其家属到监狱要求探视，亦遭拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其案在湖南省浏阳市法院开庭受审，尽管其为自己做了无罪辩护，但依然被该法院当庭以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；据悉，其代理律辩护师曾请求与其见面遭拒，其家人要求到监狱探视亦被拒绝。目前在湖南省长沙监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、齐红玉：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省双鸭山市集贤县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点左右，集贤县法轮功学员齐红玉女士在街上讲真相时，被不明真相世人诬告，被抓捕到前进派出所。下午三点多，国保大队长冯树斌等人，带着开锁人员打开齐红玉家门抄家，当晚把齐红玉送进双鸭山市看守所。后在未通知家人的情况下，集贤县法院非法对齐红玉开庭，判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省荆州市荆州区法轮功学员。荆州市荆州区法轮功学员王美卿、刘新安、仇运凤、邓永梅<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日晚上，开着汽车在马山（荆州与当阳、枝江交界处）发放法轮功资料时、被人举报，被当阳市（属湖北宜昌市管辖）草埠湖派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日当阳市法院下达了判决书：仇运凤被判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；王美卿被判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；刘新安被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；邓咏梅被判处<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因发大法真相资料被关押三十天，后又被劫持到洗脑班迫害。妻子马秀云，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年六十多岁，多次被关押、劳教。唐平顺、马秀云夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日再次被警察抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夫妻二人均被朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金四千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: lang="EN-US">9</span>日王炳程与其母亲刘朋被居住地派出所和长安公安分局抓捕，母女后被转入石家庄市第二看守所关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，桥西区法院对其母女二人均判刑<span _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省嫩江县九三农垦局荣军农场法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生。王洪霞、于桂荣<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日发放真相资料，被警察跟踪，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在于桂荣家被嫩江县公安局不法警察绑架，被关押到齐齐哈尔第二女子看守所。（这是王洪霞、于桂荣两人第二次同时遭绑架、构陷，被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，她们两人被绑架，于桂荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，王洪霞当时也被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，黑龙江省嫩江县法院判处王洪霞<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王秋萍：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">沈阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生。因修炼法轮功，王秋萍曾经被关押在马三家劳教所迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日因发放疫情周刊被一位武警恶告。送到马路湾派出所，搜走了随身带的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>千多元钱和手表、自行车和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>张封城期间的某小区通行证。由两个和平区国保大队的人连打带骂的审问，王秋萍不配合迫害，没报名，没签字，半夜逃走。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，再次被抓捕，送往和平区精神病院迫害。王秋萍被关押在精神病院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个半月多后，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被和平区国保大队、马路湾派出所警察送往沈阳市第二看守所迫害。看守所拒绝家人送衣物、存钱，更不许律师接见。王秋萍<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被关押到辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">28</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b 0pt;">、王彦东：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市绥中县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，绥中县国保大队副大队长刘唤宇等人，闯到高华家，抓捕了高华和高英姐妹，以及去串门的法轮功学员陈文艳和王彦东，抢劫了高华家的电脑、打印机等私人财物。高华被关押在葫芦岛看守所，高英被关押在葫芦岛拘留所，王彦东被关押在绥中看守所。陈文艳被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高华、高英、王彦东被构陷到绥中县检察院。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，高英回家，被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，高华、王彦东被构陷案到了葫芦岛连山检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日高华、王彦东被葫芦岛市连山法院判刑：高华<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，王彦东<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；王彦东刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">17</span>日凌晨一点多钟被长沙市开福区刑警队在其居住的出租房抓捕，并抄家构陷，关押到长沙第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获刑，她已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">30</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、邢望力：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1971</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年出生，河南省信阳市息县人，又名吴全力，维权访民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因<span lang="EN-US">7</span>岁幼子邢鉴（时名邢路路）被车祸撞成重伤，地方当局枉法处理且私分赔偿款，自此全家人走上维权道路；因逐级频繁上访，其家数人曾被当局非法拘禁、劳教、判刑等共计达<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年之久，其亦被多次关押拘禁；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因息县维权访民冯国辉在上访期间离奇死于息县农贸市场的出租屋内，邢与妻子等人在网上要求中纪委、公安部等就此事介入彻查，遂惹怒地方当局；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被息县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，指控其尿射县法院名称牌子和抗议法院对其女儿邢梅、母亲及岳母的不公判决等；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”、“敲诈勒索政府”二罪正式逮捕，关押在信阳市息县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在河南省信阳市息县法院开审，被一审以“ 敲诈勒索政府罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服立即上，不想次日竟险遭死亡，而狱方事发<span lang="EN-US">10</span>小时后才通知家人，称其在监舍窗口试图用裤子上吊自杀，被人救下时，不慎头朝下重撞头部，致其“右侧额颞叶脑挫裂伤、枕骨骨折、左侧顶部硬膜外血肿、两肺下叶挫伤、双侧胸腔积液，脑组织积水”，因未脱离危险期家属不得看望；据悉，其在看守所期间，曾屡遭酷刑折磨和牢狱虐待；后经信阳市中级法院二审裁决，“敲诈勒索政府罪”被取消，最终被以“寻衅滋事罪” 判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日刑满释放后，其夫妇因儿子车祸赔偿款遭时任管理者当局贪污，曾数度被投入狱中，遭到当局强力迫害，夫妻二人疾病缠身，无奈之下于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底前往北京寻医治病，但从北京火车站下车便被当地政府截访人员绑架、遣返、拘留，之后又被河南省信阳市息县法院以”困难救济<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>人民币”为定罪依据，以“寻衅滋事罪”将其枉判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；其不服上诉，后经由河南省信阳市中级法院二次密审，依然驳回上诉，维持原判，后送河南省信阳监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，曾因其夫妇二人于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日前往河南省罗山县灵山镇看望被当局软禁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年有余的人权律师江天勇，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又因在北京市东城区信访投诉，遂再遭北京市前门派出所警员的盘查和拘押，后移交给河南省息县警方，被处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，行政拘留期满日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转为刑事拘留；后被批捕。目前被羁押于河南省息县看守所。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2022</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，邢望力的家属首次见到该判决书：河南省信阳市息县法院认定《致社会各界人士及网友的一封求助信》系虚假信息，诽谤多名公职人员，造成社会恶劣影响，将邢望力以“诽谤罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；其不服，已提起上诉；二审正在对待中。目前被羁押于河南省息县看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/211.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/211.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">31</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、杨任涛：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1998</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，香港油尖旺区人，音响工程人员，香港逃犯条例修订草案（民间和媒体俗称“送中条例”、“逃犯条例”或“引渡条例”）反对者，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>·<span lang="EN-US">1</span>尖沙咀抗议者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因中共当局在香港推出“逃犯条例修订草案”，遭到香港民众普遍反对，遂掀起“反送中”运动，并由香港民间人权阵线发起“没有国庆，只有国殇”游行，以期在庆祝中华人民共和国成立<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年大会期间同步进行示威，由港岛铜锣湾游行至中环，向港府表达反对“逃犯条例修订草案”的要求，但却遭到港府及其港警的明确反对，并被公众集会及游行上诉委员会上诉后被驳回；不料香港官方的这一反对立场迅速激起了要求高度自治，“真普选”和“真自由”的香港本土民众的强烈反对，故有大批民众决定自我承担法律后果，并于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日国庆节起，在港多区自行发起“反对逃犯条例修订草案”抗议行动；其因响应“反送中”运动号召，故与逾千人积极参与了从尖沙嘴到油麻地一带（尤指尖沙咀警署与长乐街之间）的抗议示威，但因抗议过程中多有示威者与前来镇压的防暴警员发生了暴力冲突，遂遭防暴警员的实弹打压，最终有多人被实弹打伤和被抓捕，其中，其与何善航等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被同天以“参与暴力”为由强行拘捕，并被指控因其等参与抗议示威之时，向警方“投掷汽油弹”，并统一“身穿深色衣物、戴面罩及手持雨伞等”以图脱责，同时还与多人“在油麻地管有伸缩警棍、手铐、锤子、折刀、改装铁通、弹弓及弹珠等”，故而其行为与基本法及香港国安法相抵触，犯有“参与暴动”和“管有攻击性武器或管有物品意图损坏财产”等罪；后其<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人案被香港警方统一移送到香港区域法院；后经多次提堂庭审而未果，又被转交到香港西九龙裁判法院继续庭审；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，终被西九龙裁判法院统一宣判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年不等刑期，其中，其因被控“管有一把扳手及一把鎅刀（即割纸刀）”而被以“暴动罪”、“管有物品意图损坏或摧毁财产罪”共判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月（即<span lang="EN-US">55</span>个月），刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。目前疑似在壁屋监狱（香港新界西贡区清水湾道<span lang="EN-US">397</span>号）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/49_5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/49_5.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体;">32</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">、<a name="_Hlk165077703">于桂兰</a></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165077703;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">：</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁抚顺市望花区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁。于桂兰老人一九九七年十月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，在抚顺市顺城区葛布新地号，于桂兰告诉人们 “法轮大法好，真善忍好”时，被人举报。于桂兰被前来的警车及举报人绑架。警察将于桂兰老人拉回派出所，晚上十点多，才让老人回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，于桂兰老人去抚顺李石开发区发法轮功资料时，被望花雷锋派出所跟踪，绑架到望花雷锋派出所。四个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上，望花区雷锋派出所警察到于桂兰家，让于桂兰到望花法院去一趟。于桂兰老人到了法院，法院人员将望花检察院对她的起诉书交给了于桂兰。于桂兰老人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在望花区法院第一法庭开庭。于桂兰老人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，随即被强行关押在看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk165077748">曾跃玲</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省广州市法轮功学员。曾兴阳的妹妹，<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，湛江师范学院毕业，在培训机构任职。曾兴阳、妻子邓芳、妹妹曾跃玲，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被天河区公安分局国保和石牌派出所警察抓捕，关押到天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，海珠区法院对<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人判刑，曾兴阳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邓芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；曾跃玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。曾跃玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span
