_Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、张勤：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，家住上海市徐汇区，原是上海市胜德塑料有限公司的技术骨干，曾任总工程师、质监科科长等职务。一九九四年九月开始修炼法轮。张勤因为坚持信仰曾经两次被判刑，刑期分别为<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，还被劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张勤又遭逮捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，张勤被上海奉贤区法院庭审、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，借口是“累犯重判”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">35</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk165077823">张伟</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，家住东港市。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，丹东市委、政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”与丹东市公安局秘密策划，经过长期电话监控以及各种监控手段、跟踪监视，对丹东市公安系统统一部署，丹东国保支队警察倾巢出动，加上直属公安分局以及法轮功学员所在地公安派出所为主力，合计至少一千几百人参与此次抓捕。此次行动，东港市<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员被抓捕。张伟也遭抓捕和抄家，抢走法轮书籍、资料若干、笔记本电脑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台、几部手机。张伟被关进丹东看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，辽宁丹东地区东港市法院对<span lang="EN-US">11</span>名法轮功学员非法庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，东港市法院对法轮功学员下达判决。张伟被非法判重刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，现非法关押在辽宁女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">1</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>小队。张伟一直坚持炼功，曾多次被打骂、体罚、强制“转化”，张伟曾绝食反迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">36</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk165077875">赵作媛</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，山东省长岛县黑山乡大濠村村民。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年赵作媛、骆卫东夫妻二人在本村经营球石厂，赵作媛的母亲葛宏婵为此投资数万元。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，因和生意合伙人<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元的债务纠纷，长岛县法院查封了赵作媛价值百万余元的球石和石料，任由债权人倒卖。赵作媛一家被迫起诉至法院要求债权人赔偿损失，岂料，法院判决赵作媛一家赔偿债权人转运这些球石过程中产生的费用。为了寻求公道，赵作媛、骆卫东和母亲一家三口被迫上访维权。上访期间，夫妇二人关系破裂导致离婚。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日赵作媛被北京市丰台区公安局以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日取保释放。<span lang="EN-US"> 2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日赵作媛被绑架到鸿锦大酒店非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">1</span>天。<span lang="EN-US"> 2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日赵作媛被暴力绑架回黑山岛非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">17</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日赵作媛被网上通缉抓捕，以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日逮捕，现羁押在烟台市看守所。据北京市第二中级人民法院赔偿委员会国家赔偿决定书中显示：<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月间，有人在北京南站以打标牌、拍照，并将照片上传到境外互联网网站的手段制造影响。该案经丰台分局侦查发现，赵作媛有重大嫌疑。经丰台分局口头传唤、讯问后，以寻衅滋事罪将其刑事拘留。对赵作媛的拘留符合法律规定的条件和程序，对赵作媛所提赔偿请求不予支持。丰台看守所不许家人为其存钱、存物，导致其受凉后落下腰疼、腹痛等疾病。在暴力劫访过程中被勒脖子，造成脖子发生病变肿大，至今未愈。在非法拘禁期间手机信号被屏蔽。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，赵作媛被烟台市蓬莱区法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉：赵作媛已移送山东省女子监狱（山东济南市高新区孙村办事处<span lang="EN-US">822</span>信箱<span lang="EN-US">100</span>分箱，邮编<span lang="EN-US">250104</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，攀枝花市攀钢集团公司第二机械厂退休工人，法轮功学员。自从中共开始迫害法轮功后，钟义芳非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年钟义芳被判刑八年，于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被关押到四川省龙泉驿女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才出狱回家<span lang="EN-US">.2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月又遭中共当局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，钟义芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。她现在被迫害得出现严重的尿毒症，骨瘦如柴，肚子肿的老大，每天看守所给她打针。生命健康令人担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">38</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、陈煜：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162566522;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk125653783;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">网名张小麦，浙江省台州临海市人，基督徒，网上书店“小麦书房”负责人，良心犯。近年来，由于中共当局加大了对宗教信仰及其信徒的打压，强化了对非官方宗教书籍的严控和取缔，为了解决书源问题，其<span lang="EN-US">"</span>小麦书房<span lang="EN-US">"</span>遂代中国信徒到台湾及海外代购基督教出版物，然后通过网上书店举行销售<span lang="EN-US">;</span>因其<span lang="EN-US">"</span>小麦书店<span lang="EN-US">"</span>坚持长期销售台湾、美国宗教书籍，颇受浙江、山东、河南等省基督徒顾客欢迎，曾被上万人次点击购买，随引起浙江当局的强烈不满，并将其及其书店视为<span lang="EN-US">"</span>反华势力<span lang="EN-US">";2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其被浙江省临海市警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>抓捕刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;</span>后被以同罪由转正式逮捕，指控其在未经境内合法书号和引进许可证的情况下，通过电商网站向一万多人售出<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万多本书，涉及金额<span lang="EN-US">282</span>万，其中，<span lang="EN-US">771</span>种属境外<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法出版物<span lang="EN-US">"</span>，所以违反了刑法<span lang="EN-US">;2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被浙江省临海市法院一审以<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">20 </span>万，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日<span lang="EN-US">;</span>二审维持原判。据悉，其被判刑与书房销售王怡牧师的《福音的政变》一书有关，曾有上万购书人均遭警方查问，并被要求全部退回<span lang="EN-US"> ;</span>被捕后，所扣押的<span lang="EN-US">12864</span>本书均遭官方销毁。后于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日获假释回家。此前被羁押于浙江省临海市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/7202444.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/7202444.html</span></b></a></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"></span><span class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk162569632"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">三、本期获悉狱中<span lang="EN-US">20</span>人的动态信息（附简历）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></a></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><a name="_Hlk159665615"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、徐光、陈剑雄、何宗旺<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被判刑：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">徐光、陈剑雄、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">何宗旺、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐光：浙江杭州中国民主党人徐光先生今获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，本网获悉：浙江杭州民主党人、八九学生领袖徐光先生今获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。徐光是在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被刑事拘留的，至今已被羁押超过<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月徐光案曾一审开庭，未宣判。今日，徐光被杭州西湖区法院开庭宣判，以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源： <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/4.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/4.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐光简历：<span lang="EN-US">1</span></span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">968</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年出生于浙江省富阳市，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年毕业于杭州大学生物系，大学期间曾参与<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年及<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年学生爱国民主运动，“八九学运”杭州大学学运领袖，中国民主党浙江委员会核心成员，于<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月在家乡富阳市环保局环境监测站工作的徐光组建了“中国民主党浙江省富阳市筹委会”，是中国民主党第一个县级组织。撰写了《抓不完的中国民主党》等文章，并起草《中国民主党富阳市筹备委员会成立公开宣言》，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被杭州市抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>被逮捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日徐光被以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；出狱后的徐光仍坚守信念，抨击时弊。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日因为在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>上参加中国民主党话题的闲聊，被浙江当局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被正式逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获释，期间从未获准律师会见。后获释。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因“六四”将近，徐光收到居住区西湖区公局分局玉泉派出所的传唤单，徐光未予理睬。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，徐光在所居东山弄小区采购，途经辖区的西湖区公安分局玉泉派出所附近，正遇上派出所民警，被带进派出所，告诫徐光“六四”将近，不要有什么涉“六四”的敏感言行，强行收走了他的手机。徐光<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日去玉泉派出所，带着写着“平反六四”的纸张，抗议公安对自己迫害。当日徐光被国保刑事拘留，被抄家，后被羁押。徐光从当日绝食抗议至今仍在绝食中，鼻饲灌注维持。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>时杭州国保第二次对徐光家搜查，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日正式逮捕徐光。徐光被控的罪名为涉嫌寻衅滋事。当局指控徐光“在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年期间，在微信，脸书，电报，油管发布视频，文章，散布损害国家形象，危害国家利益的虚假信息。指控徐光在网络上寻衅滋事。”徐光认为系当局构陷，徐光称：自己作为当年杭州六四学运的参予者，每年都公开纪念“八九六四”和举牌“勿忘六四”。当局为六四维稳需要，打压中国民主党人，在六四前抓捕自己。徐光坚决要求律师做无罪辩护。现徐光关押在杭州市西湖区分局看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，徐光被杭州西湖区法院开庭宣判，以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈剑雄：湖北省赤壁市民主人士陈剑雄获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉：湖北省赤壁市民主人士陈剑雄（原名陈进新）案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日上午在湖北省通城县法院宣判，其被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">。信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/4_10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/4_10.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈剑雄（原名陈进新）简历</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年出生，湖北省赤壁市人，网名陈剑雄，“赤壁五君子”之一，南方街头运动践行者，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年以来，曾多次参与国内的围观声援活动，勇于多次举牌、拉横幅表达对民主宪政的政治要求，是南方街头运动杰出代表之一，亦因此曾多次遭到中共警方的拘留、刑拘、酷刑和强行驱赶等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曾因与袁小华、袁奉初、黄文勋等民主维权者在湖北省赤壁市宣传民主政治，而被当地警方以“煽动颠覆国家政权”为由刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾与民主维权者谢文飞在广东省佛山市街头举横幅，要求“废除一党专制，建立民主中国”，而被佛山警方再次以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，并关押在天河区看守所，备受酷刑折磨，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因参加山东曲阜薛福顺非正常死亡事件观察团奔赴曲阜追查真相，多次在曲阜遭警方殴打和驱赶；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因到黑龙江省声援“建三江律师被拘事件”，而被当警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因到武汉市与多名友人会见佛教法师徐志强，被武汉警方抓走，又被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因再次前往河南郑州参与公民声援“郑州十君子事件”，并到河南焦作市声援“张小玉夫妇杀警事件”，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方在郑州第三看守所附近抓走，且被湖北省赤壁市警方直接报检察院以涉嫌“扰乱社会公共秩序罪”执行逮捕，羁押于赤壁市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被湖北省咸宁市赤壁市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，刑满释放；出狱后，其追求民主意志弥坚；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因与维权友人袁兵、梁一鸣去赤壁市公安局国保大队投诉出狱后遭长期监控、骚扰等事宜，终因双方理念不同、争论激烈而不欢而散；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，再次被赤壁市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被赤壁市检察院正式批捕，并被羁押于赤壁看守所：<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，终被湖北省赤壁市法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，经咸宁市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刑满释放。此前在湖北省咸宁监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日陈剑雄又被当地警方刑事拘留，后被批捕<span lang="EN-US">,</span>罪名是寻衅滋事。后遭起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日开庭审理，未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日宣判，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。目前被羁押在湖北赤壁市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何宗旺：因关注叶钟惨死案遭抓捕的福建被酷刑致残的人权捍卫者何宗旺今获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，本网获悉：因关注叶钟惨死案遭抓捕的福建被酷刑致残的人权捍卫者何宗旺所谓袭警案于今天宣判，何宗旺被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/13_22.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/13_22.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何宗旺简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1964</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，福建福清市人，药材经销商，“<span lang="EN-US">9</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">‧</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">12</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">鞭炮大抓捕案”当事人，维权公民，人权捍卫者。因长期致力于为弱势群体维权发声，<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">成为中共福建当局的维稳管控对象；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾因网上转发北京金水桥事件帖子而被警方刑拘<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年起，曾因参与实地围观、<span lang="EN-US">4.29</span>苏州拜祭林昭、到郑州旁听贾灵敏案庭审，及两次赴庆安围观徐纯合案等，被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大召开前夕，被福州警方刻意以涉嫌“赌博罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，随后又以涉嫌“参与赌博罪”再被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因与多名福州维权公民迎接维权者严兴声刑满出狱，在福州第一看守所门口放鞭炮，而被福州市晋安区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；后又被以“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪”执行逮捕，羁押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，又被闽清县检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”及“传播造谣罪”起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其案在福州市闽清县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，终被该法院一审以“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；其不服上诉；后经福州市中级法院二审裁决，认为原审判决部分认定事实不清、证据不足，故撤销原判，发回重审；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，经福州市闽清县法院再次审案，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刑满释放；据悉，在潍坊看守所羁押期间遭酷刑虐待，曾被连续<span lang="EN-US">6</span>天疲劳审，关押近三个月后脊椎囊肿爆裂，导致下肢瘫痪且大小便失禁，至今仍留下后遗症。此前在福建省福清监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，叶钟的妻子李美英给何宗旺打电话，聊了叶钟死亡的事情。当天晚上何宗旺被抓捕，审讯期间发生冲突，何宗旺被处<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天行政拘留期满，后又被以袭警罪刑事拘留，送入福清市看守所，后被批捕。何宗旺身体状况极差，血压高达<span lang="EN-US">210</span>，有心梗病史，本来看守所不敢收，是公安局领导特批关押。曾经晚上病情发作，紧急抢救。目前服用降压药。原本他的脊柱落下残疾，看守所内日常生活无人照料，更加艰难。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、杨绍政、谢阳、谭兵林、黄琦、常昊、覃永沛、朱玉芳、史庭福、刘金萍、樊钧益、常玮平、陈文胜、季孝龙、高智晟、张忠顺、崔荣、张春雷<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">17</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">人狱中动态信息通报：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨绍政：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的著名民主人士、原贵州大学教授杨绍政已经被转监贵州省兴义监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的著名民主人士、原贵州大学教授杨绍政已经被转监贵州省兴义监狱，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。兴义是离贵州省会贵阳最远的贵州城市，目前还不通高铁。黔西南州州府兴义市是贵州省唯一一个没有通高铁的市州，从贵阳开车去兴义要四小时，去一趟来回要八个小时，家属探监极为不便。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/46.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/46.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨绍政简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1969</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，四川省巴中市人，成都市温江区学府尚郡暂住居民，中国农工党党员，西南财经大学经济学博士，前重庆工商大学教师，原贵州大学经济学院教授、硕士生导师和贵州大学高等教育评估与研究专家，贵州大学经济类学科首个被引进人才，中国知名经济学者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年大学毕业参加工作后，又于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年起进入贵州大学任教，被该校视为经济类学科首个引进的人才以来，一直深得该校的好评和荣耀，然之后因其经常发表令中共当局敏感和忌讳的政治言论，随屡遭贵州当局的监控与维稳打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因网发揭露中共党政人员每年耗费<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万亿元人民币等的相关信息，而被贵州大学叫停授课，且此前就曾因涉政言论而两次被贵州省公安厅约谈和被明确警告在中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大期间“闭嘴”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其被贵州大学以发表敏感言论为由正式开除；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“六四”期间，曾因其在微信群讲<span lang="EN-US">38</span>军军长徐勤先的司机披露说六四杀了<span lang="EN-US">3000-5000</span>名学生，随立刻被贵州省政法委、贵州省网信办及多名警察以“寻衅滋事”为由传唤；传唤中，遭虐待式审讯长达<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多小时，双手被戴手铐、脚镣，和固定在老虎椅子上，并被要求其衣服脱光、抽血、采集十指指纹及尿检等；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年中共“十·一”期间，曾又遭贵州省政法委控制而软禁多日；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因杨绍政频发政治敏感言论，虽遭警方警告也不停息，遂再次被贵州省贵阳市花溪区警方秘密带走。自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，知其被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政府罪”指定居所监视居住，后遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日在贵阳市中级人民法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被以煽动颠覆国家政权罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。此前被羁押在贵阳市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月杨绍政教授已被送到贵州省兴义监狱关押服刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳：被羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多的湖南人权律师谢阳狱中情况通报（<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，本网获悉：被羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多的湖南人权律师谢阳狱中情况，现在通报如下：据陈桂秋女士今天通报：“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>人权律师谢阳第二次被非法羁押第<span lang="EN-US">813</span>天。律师最近会见了他，会见情况如下：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、浓密的长发，与霍元甲、陈真发型相似。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、精神状态不错，意志坚定。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、对律师不被允许复制案卷材料不可接受。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、案件由最高法院延期几次了。长沙市公检法司从未放弃对谢阳的打击、对我们曾经美好家庭的摧毁。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/2202445.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/2202445.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳简历：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，湖南省长沙市人，天地人律师事务所和长沙京盈科律师事务所前任律师，原湖南纲维律师事务所律师，人权律师，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年正式执业以来，曾因代理多起公权力滥权案件，如山东省曲阜县薛明凯案、北京新公民运动张宝成案、河南省南乐县南乐教案、湖南省浏阳市张开华征地案等维权案件，并积极关注和参与社会维权运动（包括探访盲人律师陈光诚和声援建三江被捕律师等），而屡遭司法当局阻扰和逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾因只身前往山东省东师古村探望盲人律师陈光陈，而被地方黑恶势力殴打抢劫；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因代理一起民间借贷纠纷案，为维护当事人利益要求取得合议庭商议结果，而被湖南省律师协会罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，并被所在事务所要求解除合同和离职；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因为“山东薛家命案”作委托代理律师，而被湖南省司法厅当局带走“约谈喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因为代理湖南省浏阳市土地维权者张开华案，在出庭时遭到当地法院的野蛮阻扰；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因多次代理维权案件，而遭到湖南省律师协会变相打压，不予批准转所手续；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因其积极代理多起长沙市雨花区强制征地拆迁案件，在代理莲湖村农民征地行政诉讼时，曾遭到当地法院非法驱逐；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其代理广西南宁北部湾建材市场当事人的维权案件，曾遭到多名不明身份人员的持械群殴，致其重伤，右腿骨折，其虽报警，但当地警方却迟迟不予出警；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其在中共“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>大逮捕”中被湖南省长沙市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“扰乱法庭秩序”、“煽动颠覆国家政权”二罪指定地点监视居住，代理律师要求会见遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案在湖南省长沙中级法院开庭受审，但因其被迫当庭认罪，否认曾受酷刑，遂于当日暂获取保候审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市中级法院正式宣判：犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，但免予刑事处罚；后其虽未被判刑入狱，但仍遭长期软禁和贴身监控；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，谢阳因<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年末前往湖南省永顺县声援因发表网络言论而被强制关进精神病院的怀孕女教师李田田，遂被长沙市警方带走失联，后知被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；其住处遭查抄，许多个人物品均被损毁，两台计算机及一个保险柜被搜走；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被长沙市检察院以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”予以正式批捕。狱中遭酷刑。目前谢阳律师被羁押于长沙市第一看守所（湖南省长沙市长沙县泉塘街道远大二<span lang="EN-US">1736</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">410131</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭兵林：湖南维权人士谭兵林案开庭已一年仍未判决<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，本网获悉：湖南维权人士谭兵林案开庭已一年，依然无判决结果。谭兵林于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，至今羁押已达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个多月，开庭也已<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年了，仍未有判决结果。身为农民的谭兵林的父亲谭敦云对这种久押不判不放的情况非常气愤。他说他自己委托的律师一直不被允许会见谭兵林，后来由当地“官员”给他家庭指派了一位律师。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭父说：他已经七十多岁，依然无法退休，生病也不敢去医院，他的儿子没有做错什么。此前谭兵林曾公开呼吁免费医疗、免费教育及平等养老，并穿着印有这些标语的<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤拍照发到网上。谭父说：不知道是不是法院以此做为谭兵林的“犯罪证据”？<b>信息来源： <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_8.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_8.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谭兵林简介</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：湖南省衡阳市祁东县人，教育平权推动者，免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老（俗称“三免”）倡导者之一，维权公民，中国在押政治犯。近年来，曾因长期参与推动教育平权运动，倡导俗称“三免”的免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老的民生要求，以及以义工身份积极参与为良心犯送饭的公益活动等，而被社会正义人士和深受关怀帮助的弱势群体广为认可和赞许；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因在老家湖南省祁东县步云桥镇几处重要地段（含市集中心地段、祁东县政府门口、县人大常委会门口等地）举牌要求民生“三免”，即免费医疗、免费教育、免费养老以及其它要求，遂被当地维稳办人员诱骗至镇政府扣押，后被祁东县警方带走调查；期间，尽管刚开始时被很快就被释放，但同天下午又被祁东县警方带走并恶意扣留<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天，要求其写保证书，保证以后不上街举牌，但被其拒绝；后祁东县教育局正副局长前来与其见面，就其举牌内容中提及的教育问题与其谈判；因其坚持向教育局长当面提出<span lang="EN-US">225 </span>个教育问题，终使对方被迫承诺回去后将就其中的<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个问题进行研讨更新，届时必向其作答；然而时至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其因一直未见教育局副局长所称的“不在学校吃饭的学生可以退伙食费”之公示，遂其前往步云桥<span lang="EN-US">3</span>所学校进行调查取证，结果不仅均未看到退款公示，反而遭到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>所校方人员的驱逐和拒绝；而与此同时，却有学生家长听闻其做实地调查，就向其反映说，学校里每天都卖垃圾食品，严重影响了孩子的身体健康，但校方却为自身利益而任由其发展；鉴此，其立即特发声明，呼吁和要求教育局务必让各学校在校门之外张贴退伙食费公示，否则其将于次日恢复上街举牌；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，因其获悉在押政治犯张展在狱中因绝食抗争而致生命垂危，故而毅然在步云桥镇街头再次勇敢举牌声援，以期能引起中共当局的重视，让病重中的张展获准保外就医；正是基于以上言行，其即引起湖南省衡阳市当局极度不满，并成为需要尽快维稳打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其因故前往海南省海口市，但在海口市火车站出站时却遭到防疫人员的拦截和要求强制做核酸检测；被其拒绝后，其身份证被扣，其本人被长时间限制在火车站不准出站；后经海南公民蓝采儿等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人到火车站为其声援，才终与海口火车站方达成协议，对方不再强制其做核酸检测，但必须被警方遣送回原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因其父母被强行接种新冠疫苗，其到村委会举牌抗议，遂立遭衡阳市祁东县警方抓捕，自此失联；同天其家被查抄，其个人手机和笔记本计算机等被一并抄走；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其父获悉，其已于被抓当天被祁东县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；后遭批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日获悉其案件已经到了审判阶段。随后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年年初已经开庭，至今未判。目前被羁押于祁东县看守所（湖南省衡阳市祁东县玉合街道办事处赵坪村国道旁边。邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">421621</span>）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄琦：获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的著名人权捍卫者黄琦狱中度过其<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁生日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，本网获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日是获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的著名人权捍卫者黄琦的<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁生日，自其此次<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被抓捕，黄琦先生已狱中度过了第<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个生日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/1261.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/1261.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄琦简历：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1963</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，四川省内江市人 “六四天网”网站创办人、中国天网人权事务中心负责人，人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。因长期关注社会热点话题，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年曾成立“天网寻人事务所”，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年曾设立“六四天网”网站，并惯于在网上发表时政敏感性文章，从而累遭当局严控、传唤、刑拘和判刑；曾因言获罪，先后三次遭到警方的拘捕，且前两次都被判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因国外异议人士在其网页上发表有关<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年天安门事件的文章，而被四川成都警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被四川省成都市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；狱中曾遭法警、狱警和其他罪犯多次毒打，导致脑积水，脑萎缩，双侧脑室扩大，导水管变窄等严重疾病；出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，曾改组六四天网为中国天网人权事务中心，创办了中国大陆第一家综合性人权组织，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日荣获第六届中国人权青年奖；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因发表有关四川地震灾难问政府的报导（即网上发文揭露汶川地震出现的“豆腐渣”工程），而第二次被成都市警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被成都市武侯区法院以“非法持有国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US"> 2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日刑满释放；然而此时因在狱中长期遭受煎熬和非人待遇，已罹患肾脏绝症；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因对一份内部文件内容曝光，其第三次被四川省绵阳市警方从成都家中带走刑事拘留，自此失联，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被以“为境外非法泄露国家机密罪”正式逮捕，并被关押在绵阳看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，其案被移交四川绵阳市法院审理；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被四川省绵阳市法院一审以“故意泄露国家秘密罪”、“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”共判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年；其不服上诉，后经绵阳市中级人民法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。目前被在四川省巴中监狱服刑。据悉，黄琦狱中曾遭虐待迫害，常被犯人殴打致腿部受伤，家人所寄存款亦被狱警随意扣押；身体健康极差，有肾功能衰竭危险，患脑积水、心脏病、肺气肿和肺炎等多种严重疾患。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">常昊：云南镇雄常昊传道案将于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日开庭<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，本网获悉：云南镇雄传道人、残障人士常昊寻衅滋事案将于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点在镇雄县法院第二审判庭开庭。信息来源：</span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/2024412.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/2024412.html</span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">常昊简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">是云南省昭通市镇雄县农村的基督教家庭教会传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，常昊被镇雄县公安以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，家里的圣经、属灵书籍和福音口罩及手机电脑等都被扣押。在经过两次退侦后，被起诉至镇雄县法院，目前羁押在镇雄县看守所。检察院指控常昊“多次在互联网上发表、转发虚假信息、不当言论，引起公共秩序严重混乱，造成恶劣社会影响”。但常昊对公安机关和检察院的指控不予认可，也坚持不认罪认罚。他认为公民有言论的自由，对于任何国家机关和国家工作人员，有提出批评和建议的权利。至今，常昊已失去自由<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月多。常昊是二级残障人士，并患有糖尿病。常昊妻子姚发珍患有甲亢和腰间椎盘病。常昊母亲已经<span lang="EN-US">86</span>岁，腿脚不好，家里急需人照顾。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃永沛：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年广西人权律师覃永沛已被转监到广西黎塘监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年广西人权律师覃永沛于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日已被转监到广西黎塘监狱第一监区。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/5_10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/5_10.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃永沛简介：广西人权律师。覃永沛是<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被抓捕的，曾被严重超期羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日南宁警方十数人闯入原百举鸣律师事务所（现百永鸣法律咨询服务有限公司）办公室，将覃永沛控制并带走，同时覃的办公室被警方查封。其随即被刑事拘留。后覃永沛被指涉煽动颠覆国家政权罪于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，覃永沛涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案已由南宁市公安局侦查结束，已经移交南宁市检察院审查起诉。后不审不判。多年来，覃永沛一直以敢言着称，曾公开悬赏征集广西司法厅及公安厅厅长的犯罪证据，加上曾公开控告司法部长傅政华，因此遭到政治报复。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，覃永沛煽动颠覆国家政权案一审宣判，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日止。其不服判决提起上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，后其案二审，维持原判。此前覃永沛律师被羁押在广西自治区第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日已被转监到广西黎塘监狱第一监区。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的狱中江西维权人士朱玉芳在江西省女子监狱遭到同监犯人殴打，境况堪忧<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，本网获悉：被以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江西维权人士朱玉芳，今年在江西省女子监狱服刑期间，遭到同监舍犯人殴打，被送到医院，其在狱中境况堪忧。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/4_11.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/4_11.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳简介</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：江西萍乡的强拆维权者。曾是经营<span lang="EN-US">4</span>家店面的私营业主，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年拆迁中，萍乡市政府主要领导亲属开办的房地产公司拒不兑现拆迁协议，朱玉芳被迫走上维权之路。在维权过程中，她不仅自己维权，也积极帮助他人维权，呼吁社会公正，遂被地方政府视为重点维稳控制和打击对象，被多次截访绑架、关黑监狱、遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，朱玉芳因在北京身穿“没有腐败就没有访民”的文化衫维权，被北京警方抓走，转交给江西萍乡安源区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱后，朱玉芳一直为被枉法冤判而申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，她到江西省高级法院申诉，遭拒，遂在法院门外举牌呼吁；一周后的<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日（世界人权日），朱玉芳就被萍乡市警方抓捕，随即被以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，朱玉芳第二次被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑，这次刑期比上次更长——<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。上诉后，萍乡市中级法院二审裁决维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。朱玉芳因为被枉法判刑而申诉喊冤，结果却遭到更大打击，被加重判刑。中共当局的司法由此可见一斑。朱玉芳目前在江西省女子监狱四监区服刑。其身患多种疾病，此次又遭受监舍犯人殴打，境况堪忧，亟需关注。朱玉芳在江西省女子监狱的通讯地址：江西省南昌市新建县<span lang="EN-US">916</span>信箱<span lang="EN-US">4</span>分箱（江西省女子监狱四监区）朱玉芳，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">330100</span>，电话：<span lang="EN-US">0791-83718743</span>江西省女子监狱地址：江西省南昌市新建县长堎镇长征路<span lang="EN-US">630</span>号江西省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8 /</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk165249530"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">史庭福</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：被跨省抓捕的南京公民史庭福的律师获会见案件已经移送检察院审查起诉<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，本网获悉：被跨省抓捕的南京公民史庭福获律师会见，目前已经移送检察院审查起诉。昨日律师在阿克苏阿拉尔市看守所会见了史庭福，由于本来就身体健康就不好，被关押后的史庭福身体状况更差。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_18.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_18.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">史庭福简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">其原是南京一位争取私权利的普通访民，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁。他是一位在恶劣的环境下一步步成长为热心的维权人士，具有令中共当局恐惧的公民意识，认同三民主义与普世价值观，更是属于街头行动派的一员。他曾在南京中山陵当众喊话到访的原国民党主席的洪秀柱，希望国民党坚守民主理念；也曾现场关注南京维权人士王健被构陷案；更在苏州“<span lang="EN-US">4.29</span>”祭奠林昭时被带走。多年来，除身体力行外，史庭福先生还在网络上声援郭飞雄，为困境中的人权律师发声，在自己经济条件非常困难情况下，还资助其他更困难的维权路上的同道。此前，史庭福<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因宣讲六四真相而被控“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕案<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在南京法庭判史庭福犯寻衅滋事罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，史庭福先生出狱。史庭福于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日因帮助新疆阿克苏生产建设兵团果农维权，被阿拉尔市城区公安局抓捕随即被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日史庭福被正式批捕。史庭福现被羁押在新疆阿克苏地区阿拉尔市看守所。史庭福目前患有高血压、肺炎、哮喘病，身体一直不好，其被新疆警方跨省抓捕，境况令人担忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘金萍：黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员刘金萍女士在黑龙江女子监狱集训监区遭残酷折磨<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，本网获悉：黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员刘金萍女士在黑龙江女子监狱集训监区遭残酷折磨。黑龙江女子监狱以其经常实施酷刑折磨女犯而臭名昭著。黑龙江省佳木斯市现年<span lang="EN-US">43</span>岁的法轮功学员刘金萍女士，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在家中被郊区公安分局国保大队及长虹派出所警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬被向阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元。刘金萍上诉。佳木斯市中院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年下旬，刘金萍就被转监到黑龙江省女子监狱。自那时起，就不断传出黑龙江省女子监狱残酷折磨、迫害刘金萍的消息。最近又有消息传出刘金萍遭黑龙江省女子监狱的情况：刘金萍先是被关到集训监区五楼五组。因为她拒绝写所谓“悔过书”“保证书”“揭批书”“决裂书”，七、八个犯人在狱警的指使下对她连打带骂，逼她坐没有垫子的小板凳，从早上坐到晚上，又从晚上坐到天亮，不写“四书”就一直强迫她坐小板凳，几天几夜不让她睡。刘金萍在五组被迫害了一段时间后，又被转到六组。六组的包夹犯人强迫她坐小板凳，稍微歪一点或弯下腰，韩莉、就用脚踹她或用拳头打她，一边打一边辱骂。刘金萍绝食抵抗对她的迫害。由于刘金萍长期被迫坐小板凳，屁股已经坐出了血。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_49.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_49.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘金萍简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生。刘金萍于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在家中被警察抓捕、抄家。当地公安、检察院以涉嫌所谓“破坏法律实施”的罪名将她刑事拘留，并将构陷材料递交到向阳区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日佳木斯市向阳区法院对此开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日向阳区法院对刘金萍判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。收到判决书后，刘金萍委托亲友辩护人上诉。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，佳木斯市中院违反法律程序，剥夺亲友辩护人的权利，没有公开开庭审理就做出了驳回上诉、维持原判的终审裁定。刘金萍先是被关押在佳木斯市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年下旬，刘金萍就被转监到黑龙江省女子监狱。自那时起，就不断传出黑龙江省女子监狱残酷折磨、迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk165250201"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size:
