name="_Hlk165250171">樊钧益</a>仍不审不判<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，本网获悉： 自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被跨省抓捕，到目前已遭羁押在云南长达<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个多月的湖南省长沙市民主人士樊钧益仍不审、不判。其目前羁押在云南昆明盘龙第二看守所（地址：盘龙区二环北路<span lang="EN-US">,</span>北校场盘龙一看对面），电话<span lang="EN-US">0871</span>—<span lang="EN-US">65164083</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">650051</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/310.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/310.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">樊钧益简介</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年出生，湖南省长沙市岳麓区人，网名：<span lang="EN-US">@</span>铁子，推号：<span lang="EN-US">@fanjunyidu</span>，多项公益活动组织者及参与者，“中国国民党”忠实粉丝，网络活跃人士，“墙外信息搬运工”，长沙“同城饭醉”活动参与者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">早年，曾组织参与多项公益活动，包括关爱山区学童、定时组织探望敬老院老人及参与公益百公里志愿者活动等，故而深得资助者和维权公民称许和认可；又因其是国军后代，长期坚定支持和拥护三民主义及国民党发到墙内，再由其创建的微信群和<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传发，而屡遭长沙当局打压；曾因按月例行组织并参与“同城饭醉”活动，以及组织经常性的举牌抗议活动等，而被长沙市警方多次“喝茶”、传唤和拘留处罚；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因参与长沙同城公民七月聚餐后举牌声援<span lang="EN-US">709</span>律师和公民，并将举牌照片发到网上，而立遭长沙市岳麓区警方约谈“喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因将“美国之音”网站的文图信息转发到微信群组，再次遭岳麓区警方传唤做笔录，其家被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因举牌要求中共结束一党专政，允许人民在推特发表言论，而被岳麓区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-29</span>日，又因公民聚餐后举牌抗议中共花纳税人的钱举行大阅兵，而被岳麓区警方以“扰乱公共秩序”罪由再次行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其突然被云南省警方跨省抓捕，次日（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日）被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，自此失联；对其被抓，外界曾一度怀疑与“六四”将至，当局恐其会有所动作，以及其近期网络言论和在微信群立转发内容有关，其被持续拘押不放；其目前羁押在云南昆明第二看守所第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>所（盘龙区二环北路<span lang="EN-US">,</span>北校场盘龙一看对面），电话<span lang="EN-US">0871</span>—<span lang="EN-US">65164083</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">650051</span>。迄今，因云南警方拒不答复外界对其案情的问询，而其家人又因恐遭警方威胁而选择对外缄默不语，故其更多信息缺详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk165250709">常玮平</a>：获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的著名人权律师常玮平今在狱中度过其<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁生日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，本网获悉：今天是著名人权律师常玮平先生<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁生日，这是他在狱中度过的第四个生日。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日常玮平律师被以颠覆国家政权罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现在陕西省渭南监狱（陕西省第二监狱）服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/3640.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/3640.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">常玮平简历</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，陕西省宝鸡市凤翔县城关镇周家门前村人，原陕西立刚律师事务所执业律师，人权律师，人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾就读于重庆大学；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，通过一系列的律师资格自修和考试，最终获取律师执业资格证，后在陕西立刚律师事务所成为正式律师；工作期间，不仅曾代理多起公益诉讼（含艾滋歧视、乙肝歧视、性别歧视等）案件，亦曾代理过多起诸如“无锡<span lang="EN-US">4</span>·<span lang="EN-US">13</span>寻衅滋事案”、“无锡访民王金娣寻衅滋事案”、“南京王健寻衅滋事案”等敏感人权及弱势群体维权案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因此而被陕西宝鸡司法局停业<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>个月；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22 </span>日，其律师资格证被当地律师事务所注销；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，在停业期满后，其基本处于无法在其他律师事务所获得工作机会的状态，因其曾在陕西省境内与至少<span lang="EN-US">10</span>家律师事务所接洽，但皆不顺利，或即将签约时临时变卦，或虽签约后又突然解除合约；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因参加了一个与多名维权律师和异见人士在厦门的非正式私人聚会，后因被中共官方知晓后定性为“厦门聚会案”，多人遭严打狠抓，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其亦被陕西省宝鸡市警方跨省抓走，并被以“危害国家安全”为由指定居所监视居住；后被取保候审，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又因对外发视频称其在拘押期间，遭受酷刑，即每天（<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时<span lang="EN-US">/</span>次）都把他绑在一种叫做“老虎凳”的刑具上，连续审问<span lang="EN-US">16</span>次，致其右手拇指到食指至今都毫无知觉，且在取保获释后仍受到严密监视等，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，随再次被陕西省宝鸡市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被宝鸡市检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在陕西省宝鸡市凤县法院秘密开庭，其妻子前往要求参加旁听，遭警方恶意围堵；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，终被宝鸡市凤县法院一审以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。此前被羁押于宝鸡市凤县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被转监到陕西省渭南监狱（陕西省第二监狱）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">12/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈文胜：湖南衡阳基督徒<a name="_Hlk165250823">陈文胜</a>案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日开庭 </span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日：庭审<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在上午九点开始，十点半左右结束。没有当庭宣判。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_53.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_53.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈文胜简介</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，湖南省衡阳市石鼓区人，住衡阳市石鼓区西湖一村<span lang="EN-US">13</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">507</span>户，基督徒，湖南衡阳小群教会信徒，街头传道人，中国在押良心犯。早年曾吸毒成性十余年，后因在戒毒所听到福音而成为基督徒，并凭信心而除掉了毒瘾，故而自此致力于广传基督教福音；曾因经常举着写有“荣耀救主”、“悔改信靠得救”的十字架独自上街宣传，或与教会其他基督徒一起走街串巷，到城市闹市区（甚至到过西藏）传福音，随屡遭当局打压，多次被警方警告、威胁和被关押在衡阳市拘留所，甚至一年之中竟有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾因到广西壮族自治区宣传基督教福音，而被南宁市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因上街传福音，而被湖南省衡阳市石鼓区警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，因与另一基督教信徒一起先后在衡阳市商业步行街附近和中医医院附近，利用喇叭、广播播放及发福音单张等方式宣传基督教，而被衡阳市蒸湘区警方以“扰乱社会秩序”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因与其母为跨农历新年传福音，而被衡阳市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；之后，因其继续走街串巷传福音，而在该年又曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因到浙江省传福音，而被辖区警方跨境抓捕，后被指定居所监视居住于西湖山庄，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天后，才在轮番轰炸般的约谈之后予以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因其到云南向少数民族朋友传福音，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，即被云南省文山壮族苗族自治州文山市警方拦截，且被移交给衡阳市警方遣回原籍；获释后，其接续外出传福音，甚至向国保警方和当地街道办事处工作人员等传福音；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其到湖南省益阳市安化县传福音，被衡阳市政法委、统战部及国保警方联合跨区抓回，次日被衡阳市青山派出所警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其重获自由，但释放当天又去上街传福音；据悉，其妻子、儿媳及孙女等家人因受牵连，曾遭当局多次恐吓和威胁，被要求务必说服、阻止其外出传福音，否则不仅儿媳会被单位开除公职，而且其孙女也会在将来不能考取国家公务员与教师等工作；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因在街头传福音被衡阳市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，期满后旋即又被以涉嫌“组织、资助非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被正式批捕。现羁押于衡阳市衡东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">13/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙：著名人权捍卫者季孝龙案二审维持<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的原判<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，本网获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，上海第一中院就著名人权捍卫者季孝龙案作出二审判决——维持一审<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的判刑结果。季孝龙于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日因替封城时的上海人民发声而遭抓捕，一审被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。季孝龙不服判决依法上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日季孝龙涉寻衅滋事案二审开庭。两位辩护律师为他做了无罪辩护。季孝龙在最后陈述中，指出从侦查开始对他的迫害就没停止过，看守所中不给他配眼镜，不让他看书，不给他治牙，自己的基本权利得不到保障；自己的被捕，完全是因为他在疫情期间为民请命，给李强发公开信所致。他的最后陈述被法官粗暴打断。他被带出法庭时高喊：你们都是罪人！<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/46_19.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/46_19.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，江苏省张家港市人，张家港市杨舍镇名都花苑居民，基督徒，维权公民，民主人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因宣传民主理念而被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由传唤，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，并在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写宣传语“大病治不起，习胖狂撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时毕！打倒共产党。还政于民，结束民众苦难。推翻习核心，拒走文革路”等字句，短时间内响应者众多，随于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被送到指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪由转正式逮捕，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被上海市浦东新区检察院起诉至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后送上海市白茅岭监狱七监区服刑；据悉，羁押期间，警方曾多次以让其“死亡”和用寒冷气温逼迫其认罪，致其身体健康虚弱且生病吐血；其家属曾送羽绒服和《圣经》书籍亦遭拒收；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刑满获释；同年上海封城，其为上海市民持续发声。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，再次被上海市梅园新村派出所警察从家中带走，后被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，又被浦东新检察院以同罪名正式批捕，后季孝龙于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被起诉。后已经开庭，未宣判。最终于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被一些寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前被羁押于浦东新区看守所（上海市浦东新区华益路<span lang="EN-US">351</span>号，邮政编码<span lang="EN-US">: 201210</span>）。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">14/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高智晟：被强迫失踪已近<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的著名人权律师高智晟先生迎来其<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁生日 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，本网获悉：自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被中共当局强迫失踪，至今已近<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的著名人权律师高智晟先生，在今天迎来其<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁生日。长达近<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的漫长时间里，高智晟律师杳无音讯、生死不明，高智晟妻子耿和女士不断发出强烈呼声，愿高智晟早日回家、早日团聚。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/760.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/760.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高智晟简介：<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，陕西省榆林市佳县人，著名维权律师，曾被中国司法部选为“中国十佳律师”，被誉为“中国良心”，异见人士，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起开始替弱势群体维权打官司，曾处理过多宗民间维权案件；自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底起，开始多次上书中共当局高层，要求改变对法轮功等群体的非法处理手段，并参与对法轮功学员器官遭当局活摘指控的调查；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，与妻子公开宣布退出中国共产党；因其勇于为当局认定的敏感性案件（注：含法轮功信仰者、基督教徒以及与官员发生纠纷的底层农民和私营企业家）辩护，故而曾多次受到中共当局以黑社会手段的严重骚扰、打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其执业执照被当局吊销，且被秘密绑架，遭近<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的酷刑；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其被突然失联，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月才被释放返京，之后又因接受了美联社采访，遂被再度失联，直至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，家属才从新华社报导中的获悉，其已被北京法院收监逮捕，接续服刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，刑满出狱，但出狱后仍被软禁在陕北榆林老家。因其曾在狱中长期遭酷刑折磨和被单独囚禁遭非人虐待，导致牙齿脱落，健康欠佳。其要求治牙看病，但一直遭拒。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，因其秘密撰写书籍《<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，起来中国》在台湾正式印刷出售，且因该书主要涉及中共当局对其长期绑架、囚禁和施以酷刑等，及其从信仰角度看中共<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年将会灭亡和对<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年后的中国未来宪政民主化展望等三大内容，遂令中共当局十分恐惧恼怒，对其监控愈加严密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，高智晟在山西维权人士李发旺、邵重国等人帮助下逃离陕西老家到山西躲藏准备看牙医，但<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被警方搜捕到带走。此外，高智晟一直没有消息，北京、陕西和山西当局都否认羁押高智晟。自高智晟律师<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭中共当局强迫失踪至今已进入第七个年头，中共当局对高智晟不审不判，对其亲属的追问不做任何回答和解释，对国际社会的关注和抗议完全置之不理。中共当局对高智晟律师的人权侵害已经到了随心所欲、丧心病狂的地步。目前高智晟被秘密关押的地点不详，生死不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张忠顺：因“厦门公民聚会案”遭羁押的山东烟台人权捍卫者张忠顺的案情通报<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，本网获悉：近日了解到，张忠顺家属曾试图为张忠顺委托律师，但办案警察对家属说张忠顺有法援律师，说张不希望家人管他的事情。警察屡次对家属提到不要管张忠顺，也不要对外提及张忠顺的事情。因家属无法见到亦无法得到张忠顺本人的任何只言片语，无法了解张真实情况和真实想法。张忠顺目前被羁押在山东临沂市临沭县看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_20.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_20.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张忠顺简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东烟台的人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月上旬，许志永、丁家喜等<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余名维权律师和人权捍卫者在厦门聚会，张忠顺是参加者之一。为此，他于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被中共当局的“<span lang="EN-US">12.13</span>专案组”以“颠覆国家政权”为名监视居住，近半年后获释。此后，因为给许志永、丁家喜的辩护律师出具证言，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张忠顺第二次被山东烟台警方以同案同罪名监视居住，其住所再次遭到搜查。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，张忠顺被转押到山东临沂市临沭县看守所刑事拘留。目前，张忠顺已被山东临沂检察院移送法院起诉，据悉尚未有律师介入。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">崔荣：获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月辽宁灯塔市法轮功学员崔荣狱中遭虐待<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月辽宁灯塔市法轮功学员崔荣狱中遭虐待。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/36_21.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/36_21.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">崔荣简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省辽阳市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓辽阳市公安局捕，被关押在辽阳市看守所。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后转监到辽宁省第二女子监狱四监区，因她坚持信仰，拒绝“转化”，监狱就不让她家人探视，也不许她买生活日用品。她每天被逼做繁重的奴工生产，从早上七点干到晚上七点，不给吃饱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">17/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春雷：贵阳仁爱归正教会长老<a name="_Hlk165265350">张春雷</a>案辩护律师多次申请阅卷遭拒，贵阳中院法官说等快判时会通知律师阅卷</span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，本网获悉：近日，被控“煽动颠覆国家政权”和<span lang="EN-US">"</span>诈骗”罪”的贵阳“仁爱归正教会”长老张春雷的辩护律师发布信息，反映其多次致电贵阳中院法官、申请阅卷均遭拒，被以“座机信号不好”等各种荒唐理由推诿，法官甚至说要等到快判时再通知律师阅卷。贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷案于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月一审开庭，至今已近一年半。从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被刑拘至今，张春雷长老更是被羁押了三年零一个月，从<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁关到<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁依然没有判决结果。严重超期羁押！<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_24.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_24.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春雷简历：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>贵州省人，基督徒，贵阳市仁爱归正家庭教会主要组建人，教会带领人、长老，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》首批签名人之一，中国在押良心犯。早年，曾因笃信耶稣基督，为广传基督教福音而与人共同组建了不从中共“三自教会”的“仁爱归正教会”；起初，该教会仅有几十会众，但在其不懈努力和事工（即神职人员在教会里所做的服务）带领下，因能热情广泛接待南来北往的信徒，故而在后来的国度事工中起到和发挥了重要的作用；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因积极参与由四川成都王怡牧师发起的《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》的首批联署签名，随遭贵阳当局的严管监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其教会被贵阳市南明区民族宗教事务局突然取缔，并被指称，因其等一行人“未经批准，擅自以‘仁爱归正教会’名义在南明区中天商务港设立宗教场所，组织、举行宗教活动，接受宗教性捐献，违反《宗教事务条例》相关规定，责令停止宗教活动，拆除相关设施和标识”，最终致使其及教会信徒在失去会堂后只能在餐厅、酒店进行主日敬拜；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因在当地某酒店举行主日聚会，而被数十名宗教局人员及警方先后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次连手冲击，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被封门，敬拜所用的十字架被强摘，其计算机等用品被查收；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因其教会新租房屋的房东再次被当局威胁，故而其被逼无奈只得再次从新租的房屋搬走；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其教会有十数名信众在参加小组学习时被突然闯入的贵阳市南明区民宗局人员和警方带走，遂其赶到派出所与警方交涉要人，不料竟遭粗暴野蛮对待，并被以“非法经营社团”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天；拘留期满时，又被贵阳市云岩区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被贵阳市云岩区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其妻子、儿子受牵连曾遭警方长时讯问且其妻遭虐待，教会多位同工成员亦遭抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其代理律师数次要求会见均受阻，被告知其“因涉嫌危害国家安全，在侦查期间未得到办案单位允许的情况下，禁止律师会见”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初遭起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日开庭，未宣判。目前被羁押于贵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四、</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本期新增被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人名单及简历<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">胡卫明、<a name="_Hlk165333231">覃伟进</a>、孙承浩<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><a name="_Hlk165246563"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡卫明</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南村镇银行女储户。胡卫明因维权在除夕<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被河南警方遭刑事拘留，其老父亲于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日含恨去世，河南村镇银行民营企业家储户联合体发讣告愤怒谴责河南当局，并公开追索迫害河南村镇银行储户的河南当局责任人的犯罪证据和线索。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_13.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_13.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃伟进：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广西覃通律师事务所主任，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年大学本科毕业、法学士，全国法院干部业余法律大学教师。曾在法院的经济庭、民庭、刑庭、少年庭工作，担任过法官、庭长，后成为专职律师。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年中共当局打压维权律师的“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>事件”后，刑辩律师举步维艰。覃伟进曾多次声援遭到不公正对待的其他刑辩律师，如<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年“广西律师吴良述在南宁青秀区法院立案不成遭法警殴打事件”、“四川律师詹肇成、刘勋被控妨害作证案”、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“广东维权律师隋牧青被吊证事件”，覃伟进都参与了联名声援。覃伟进律师在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被柳州市公安局柳江分局以“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”为名刑拘。覃伟进律师具体表达了什么言论而被当局以“煽动”治罪，目前尚不清楚，但“煽动”罪通常是中共当局打压言论自由的一项口袋罪。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_36.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/blog-post_36.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><a name="_Hlk165266287"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙承浩</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃张掖孙承浩牧师被以涉嫌“组织他人偷越国边境罪”于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日抓捕，目前仍被羁押，具体案情尚不明了，需要进一步了解。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/20231215.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">3</span>个月：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">王桂霞、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吴树玲、杨素霞、</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜晓燕</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：或名姜晓艳，黑龙江哈尔滨市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，家住哈尔滨市双城区，一九九九年前开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，哈尔滨市公安局、双城区公安分局警察抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">56</span>名哈尔滨法轮功学员，后其中<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被劳教，六人遭判刑，姜晓艳被判重刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。在黑龙江省女子监狱姜晓燕被迫害致奄奄一息，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年保外就医。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，姜晓燕再次被收监入狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年正月，姜晓燕的家人去探监，狱方称姜晓燕没有“转化”不能探视，家人据理力争，狱方才勉强同意。这是家人五年来第一次见到姜晓燕，看到她的牙齿几乎掉光了。据悉，姜晓燕现被单独关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/14.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，邓道恒被转监到嘉州监狱。自从邓道恒被劫入嘉州监狱后，近四年过去了，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，家属接到嘉州监狱人员通知，称邓道恒已在重症监护室抢救。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日上午九点多，家属才只能从视频里和邓道恒见了一面。邓道恒很瘦，几乎是瘦得皮包骨了，说是“糖尿病并发症”。但是，目前家人既不能到他身边护理，也无法办理“保外就医”，仍没有监狱和相关公安的回复。人命关天，家人心急如焚。其刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，王朝杰被文峰区国保警察抓捕，关押到安阳市看守所。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，王朝杰被构陷到安阳市法院，进入庭审阶段。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，安阳市法院于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年对王朝杰判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。安阳市法院直接从王朝杰的公积金中扣押罚金，余额逼迫家属补齐到<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元整。王朝杰于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被转监到郑州新密市监狱，现在他被关押在新密市监狱九监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">大连市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，孔庆平被李家街派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时候释放，对她监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底，警察强迫孔庆平去沙河口区李家街派出所，逼迫她写“放弃修炼法轮功的保证书”。孔庆平不配合，被关了一天一夜。派出所警察向家人勒索一万元“保证金”后，以“取保候审”形式放她回家。一年后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，警察以“取保候审”到期为由，要孔庆平再去派出所。孔庆平为了躲避进一步的迫害，被迫离家，流离失所。孔庆平在外流离失所一年半后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午三点左右，李家街派出所警察跟踪孔庆平的家人，至孔庆平在庄河市的出租屋，抓捕了孔庆平。随即孔庆平被关押到大连市姚家看守所，家人一直不得探视。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，大连市甘井子区法院对孔庆平开庭，并对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。其不服判决，依法上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被大连市中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。沈绍春牧师的父母都是基督教的传道人，其早年即皈依基督教，就读神学院，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年开始全职传教，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年在缅甸佤邦创办“活水小学”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">47</span>岁，吉林省辽源市西安区辽源裕丰粮食收储职工，家住吉林省辽源市西安区灯塔乡成山村。梁桂娟于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日宣判：梁桂娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">耿迎凤：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">南京靖江市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1938</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">86</span>岁。一九九六年，耿迎凤开始修炼法轮功，一九九九年七月中共当局疯狂迫害法轮功后，耿迎凤坚持宣讲法轮功，因此，多次被警察抓捕关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，时年八十岁的耿迎凤再被靖江市法院判刑三年。因为身体原因，泰兴监狱拒绝接收她，耿迎凤老人被“取保”，还剩余两年非法刑期。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，耿迎凤等四位老年女法轮功学员在一起阅读法轮著作《转法轮》时，被南京市江宁区警察抓捕到高新园派出所。之后，耿迎凤被南京市雨花区法院开庭，在原来剩余两年刑期的基础上，再次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚款人民币三万元。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年中秋节后，耿迎凤被收监到常州女子监狱，被执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年刑期，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，刑满那时耿迎凤将<span lang="EN-US">87</span>岁。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; lang="EN-US">30</span>日结束冤狱。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日下午五点，肖崐和姐姐肖洋在家中楼下被哈尔滨市阿城区国保大队警察抓捕，抄家。警察将肖崐、肖洋劫持到阿城区公安分局，被审讯到半夜。后半夜肖洋被放回。肖崐则被警察关押到哈尔滨市第二看守所。肖崐对警察的一切要求都不配合，她不“转化”、不签字、零口供，之后被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李学贻：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">甘肃临夏市法轮功学员，男。李学贻的父亲李建魁，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁，甘肃核工业地质<span lang="EN-US">212</span>大队退休职工，早年修炼法轮功，一九九九年七月二十日中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，李建魁一家人都遭受了迫害。李建魁老人曾多次被中共绑架、非法关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受酷刑迫害，至今留有严重脑淤血后遗症，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，李建魁老人再次被绑架到临夏县看守所关押，被判刑，关押在兰州监狱。李学贻（李学怡），小名天增，从小就因其父修炼法轮功遭株连遭受迫害，曾被抓捕、劳教，遭酷刑折磨，曾被殴打至耳朵失聪。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年李学贻在陕西省榆林市榆神工业园区工作，时年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日因他被发放法轮功宣传资料，被榆林市公安局抓不，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。李学贻目前仍然被非法关押在榆阳区看守所，据说要被非法关押到陕西渭南监狱去。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/36_16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵国坤：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年生，她和她的父亲赵旭东、母亲李艳、哥哥赵国兴都于一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。母亲于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被迫害离世，时年<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁。她的父亲于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年含冤离世，时年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日晚，赵国坤与父亲赵旭东（时年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁）和哥哥赵国兴被闯入家中的吉林市国保大队、哈达湾派出所、兴华派出所警察抓捕。赵国坤与父亲赵旭东关押到吉林市看守所。赵国兴第二天获释回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，赵国坤在被拘留十三天后从吉林市看守所获释回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底，赵旭东老人在被关押近一个月后从吉林市看守所获释回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，赵国坤收到昌邑区检察院的“起诉书”、“量刑建议书”与昌邑区法院的所谓“监视居住决定书”。父亲赵旭东的精神与身体状况开始每况愈下。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，赵旭东老人在精神和肉体双重迫害下含冤离世。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚，赵国坤再次被抓捕，后关押到吉林省长春女子监狱，才由监狱通知了家属。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，赵国坤被秘密庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">2012</span>年二月，秦秀娟在武汉给儿子看孩子期间，被武汉市公安局青山分局武抓捕，后秦秀娟被武汉市青山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，后被关押到武汉市女子监狱迫害。秦秀娟老太太于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因张贴“法轮大法好，真善忍好”不干胶，被武汉市轨道交通管理公安分局三金潭派出所警察入室抓捕，关押在武汉市第一看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初获悉：秦秀娟被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span 0pt;">山东省青岛市下辖平度市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁。家住平度市凤台街道店前村，她于一九九九年正月开始修炼法轮功。在中共自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年开始对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，李丽多次被绑架、关押，曾一次被劳教、三次被判刑，累计陷冤狱十三年半。狱中曾遭残忍酷刑折磨。李丽女士于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被国保警察从家中抓捕、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，她在青岛普东看守所被青岛市黄岛区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年三月下旬获悉：李丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省绥化市兰西县法轮功学员，男。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在家中被警察抓捕，随即被安达市检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金一万元。刑期至：<span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">藏族，青海省果洛藏族自治州班玛县人，青年歌手。果洛华丹平时喜欢音乐，尤其马头琴弹唱。去年他在中国社交媒体“快手”上发布一首名为“思念母亲”的歌曲，受到藏人民众的喜欢，他的快手账号上拥有<span lang="EN-US">98000</span>多粉丝，而他最后一次更新快手是在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。后获悉其遭抓捕，此时应是其被抓捕的时间。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月《西藏之声》报道果洛华丹因演唱的歌曲内容“歌颂与维护西藏的尊严”并被秘密判处了<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。其家人连法院的判决通知书都没有收到，只是被口头告知他遭判三年有期徒刑的消息。目前他被关押在班玛县监狱。刑期应至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省唐山市法轮功学员，女。与北秦皇岛市抚宁区法轮功学员王永花女士是儿女亲家母。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初在天津滨海新区儿子女儿家被当地警察从家中抓捕，一直被关押在当地看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，王永花与张茂霞分别被判刑三年，其现在仍被关押在天津滨海新区看守所，不许家属会见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王永花：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">或名王咏花，河北秦皇岛市抚宁区法轮功学员，女，生于一九六三年十一月，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月二十日中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，经常遭受迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年王永花和丈夫分别被冤判三年半和三年，王永花被送入石家庄女子监狱，丈夫被送入冀东监狱，在监狱里遭受了非人的折磨，王永花曾经被长期的吊铐。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初在天津滨海新区儿子女儿家被当地警察从家中抓捕，一直被关押在当地天津滨海新区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张淑芬：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在中共发动对法轮功学员的疯狂迫害后，张淑芬曾多次被绑架、抄家，被拘留、劳教、扣除工资，关押期间被警察殴打，遭老虎凳、电棍、野蛮灌食等酷刑折磨；在劳教所被迫做奴工，狱警为了逼迫她“转化”，长时间不让她睡觉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，张淑芬因宣讲法轮功被向阳分局警察抓捕、抄家，后被判刑一年半，被关押到吉林省女子监狱迫害。张淑芬于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被辽源市泰安公安分局警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，辽源市龙山区法院其庭审，并于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日宣判：张淑芬被判刑<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李秀珍又被警察抓捕、抄家，并被批捕。此后，潍坊市坊子区公、检、法对李秀珍实施司法迫害，没有通知家人，对她进行秘密庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日才获知，李秀珍被判刑三年。李秀珍已于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/26.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">苏春风：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北沧州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚，河北沧州市法轮功学员苏春风、胡秀梅、刘在云、侯树元<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人在新华区邓家屯村西口，被跟踪而至的新华区公安分局国保大队警察抓捕。后刘在云、胡秀梅、侯树元被关押沧州市看守所，苏春风因身体原因，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被“取保候审”回家。后四人均被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，苏春风在家中再次被新华分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，经三次体检，在体检不合格的情况下，苏春风被强送看守所，看守所非法收押。苏春风被沧州市看守所迫害出重病，无法正常排尿，被下尿管维持，在看守所中生活难以自理，身体状况堪忧。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日苏春风、侯树元、刘在云和胡秀梅<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人遭运河区法院非法判刑：侯树元、刘在云遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金一万元；苏春风、胡秀梅遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金五千元。苏春风刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙万良：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省铁岭市昌图县法轮功学员。因宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，昌图县国保大队闯入孙万良家中，把孙万良抓捕。孙万良在被抓捕后，他八十三岁的老父亲因惊吓、担忧儿子，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日去世。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，律师会见孙万良时得知他在看守所被犯人踢断一根肋骨，在重伤期间还被单独关进一个间室坐板。家属非常气愤，控告主要责任人，要求依法追究昌图县看守所所长涉嫌虐待罪。孙万良于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在昌图县法院被开庭，律师为他做了无罪辩护，有理有据。最终，孙万良被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/2.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 0pt;">高秀花：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东青岛市法轮功学员，女，家住青岛市黄岛灵山卫办事处，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年已年过七旬。高秀花老人<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底发放法轮功资料时被人举报，她被当地灵山卫派出所警察抓捕。因高秀花年纪过大及身体原因当天晚上回到家中。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日晚八点，灵山卫派出所三名警察上门说去派出所填资料一会就能回家。高秀花到了派出所，警察说因为以前放资料被举报，黄岛法院已经批捕她了。随即，高秀花被关押在灵山卫派出所。后高秀花被送医院，检查出半个肺部没有功能，肺结核、心脏病、高血压等症状，但仍被强行关押到普东看守所。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日高秀花在普东看守所，被庭审判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何世国：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省邯郸市永年区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年生，家住邯郸市永年区（原永年县）小龙马乡北护驾村。中共迫害法轮功后，何世国因坚持自己的信仰，多次被中共绑架、关押，他曾三次被劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，何世国被邯郸市公安局国保大队、永年分局国保大队联合抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，其被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月后，何世国已被转监到唐山冀东监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/16_16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王桂霞：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年开始修炼法轮功，王桂霞因传播法轮功，曾两次中共被抓捕，关押在辽宁女子监狱、锦州市看守所，遭受过残暴酷刑折磨。王桂霞老太太因传法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被锦州市公安局凌河分局石桥子派出所警察抓捕，后被所谓“取保候审”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，王桂霞被秘密绑架，家属得到通知时她已被关押到锦州市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王桂霞被凌海市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被构陷到凌海市检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被起诉到凌海市法院。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初获悉：王桂霞老人被锦州市下辖凌海市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/13_26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">45/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴树玲：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市开平区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年左右生，现年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多岁，原来在唐山市第四十六中学后勤工作，一九九六年开始修炼法轮大法。吴树玲女士在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月因宣讲法轮功遭抓捕，一直被关押在唐山市第一看守所。之后，家里就再没得到她任何消息，直到<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日她给家里写了信，才简单了解到她于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。吴树玲目前被羁押在唐山市第一看守所<span lang="EN-US">803</span>室。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/1.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西汉中市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁，家住陕西省汉中市汉台区培德街。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年开始修炼法轮功。因发放法轮功光盘，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，杨素霞，经由汉中市汉台区公安、检察院、法院的合伙欺骗和暗箱构陷，被判刑一年。随即抓捕，并关押在汉台区看守所。近期得知，三月底，杨素霞老人已被转监到陕西省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span
